 vahiin cadmium 0
 38 mg \ kg, chromium up to 796 mg \ kg

 rajdhani dilli ke buraadi ke sant nagar ilaake main ek hi ghar main 11 logon kii maut main bitate vakt ke saath kai angal saamne aa rahe hai
 The family's mass suicide has affected people across the country
 vahiin maamle kii jaanch main ek ke baad ek kai rahasyamayi baaten or saboot bhi mil rahe hai

 is bich krime branch ke sutara ne bataaya ki donon registers main chote bhai lalit kii hand riting lag rahi he, jisaki furniture kii dukaan thi

 ghar ke peeche 11 pipe kaa rahasy?jaanch aage badi to bhaatia parivaar ke ghar ke peeche 11 pipe mili, jisamen se chaar pipe sidhe hai or saat mude hai

 kya andhvishwaas main puure parivaar ne kii khudakushi?dilachasp he ki jaanch team ko ghar se do register mili hai jisamen kuch aisi chijen likhi hai jo dheron sawaal khadey karti hai
 Every single thing written in the register corresponds to the incident
 register main likhaa he ki pattiyaan achche se baandhani hai
 It is worth noting that barring one of the bodies recovered from the house, everyone had bandages on their eyes
 register main likhaa he ki saat din baad lagaataar puja kerani he
 If someone comes into the house, it is written in the register to choose the next day on Thursday or Sunday
 dilachasp he ki vaardaat ravivaar kii raat hui
 It is written in the register that if Babbe (grandmother) cannot stand, she can lie down in a separate room
 bebbe shaayad us bujurg mahila ko kaha gaya he jinaki laash alag kamare main baraamad kii gai
 It is written in the register that the use of dim light is to be done
 register main likhaa gaya he ki munh kii pattee ko roomaal se dabl kar lenaa
 It is written in the register that action has to be done between 12 to 1 in the night
 kya kisi tantra mantra ke chakkar main tha puraa parivaar?prashasan ne krime branch ko jo report saunpi he usamen ye kaha gaya he ki parivaar behad andhvishwasi tha or tantra-mantra ke chakkar main tha

 kisi baba ke chakkar main tha puraa parivaar?jab baat andhvishwaas main jaan dene kii ai to jaanch team ne apane ghode daudaaye

 World Health Day 2019: 7th April is celebrated as 'world Health Day' worldwide
 world health orgenigeshan (WHO) har saal 7 april ko world health de kaa aayojan karata he
 Its purpose is to make people aware of their health
 saal 1948 main WHO ne pehali world health assembly kaa aayojan kiya tha
 After this, World Health Day started being celebrated every 7 April from the year 1950
 iske tahat har saal vaishvik str par swasthya se judi theme chuni jaati he or use vaishvik or kshetreey str par lagu karne kii koshish kii jaati he
 The theme of World Health Day this year is 'universal Health Coverage'
 aaie world health de ke maukey par aapako bataate hai healdi rahane ke kuch khaas tips-1
 Drink more water - To stay healthy, drinking plenty of water is very important
 bharpoor maatra main pani pine se sharir sahi tareeke se kaam karata he
 Every person must drink at least 2 liters of water throughout the day
 pani pine se sharir hydrateed rahata he or sharir se toxins baahar nikal jate hai
 2
 fal or subjiyon kaa adhik seven karen-fal or subjiyon main bharpoor maatra main vitamin, minerals or fibre maujuud hota he
 To stay healthy, you should consume about 5 fruits throughout the day
 subah ke naashte main falon kaa zeus lenaa phydemand hota he
 At the same time, apple and watermelon etc
 can be taken as snacks
 3
 Reduce the amount of sugar and salt in the diet - Excess of salt intake in the diet can cause blood pressure problems as well as risk of heart disease
 vahiin, chini khaane kaa swaad to badhaati he lekin sehat ko kaaphi nuksaan pahunchaati he
 This has been confirmed in many studies as well
 isliye diet main chini or namak kaa kam se kam istemaal karen
 4
 vajan ko control main rakhen-healdi lifestil ke liye vajan ko control main rakhana bahut jaruri he
 Increased weight knocks out many serious diseases
 inamen pramukh rup se diabetes, heart atake or cancer jaisi ghaatak bimariyon kaa khatra bad jaataa he
 So to stay healthy always follow healthy diet and keep your weight under control
 5
 Exercise - Exercise is very important to reduce weight or to be more physically fit
 eksrasij karne se calories bern hoti he
 The heart remains healthy as well as the circulatory system of the body works properly
 eksrasij karne se mansapeshiyaan bhi majboot hoti hai
 Make the habit of exercising at least 150 minutes a day a part of your routine
 6
 Get plenty of sleep - To stay healthy, sleeping for 7-8 hours is very important
 acchhee sehat ke liye ek acchhee or sukun-bhari neend behad ahm hoti he
 Getting less sleep can hurt your health in many ways
 neend kii kami ke kaaran diabetes, stroke or motaape kaa shikaar hone kii sambhaavna sabase zyada hoti he
 Health experts believe that, by getting plenty of sleep, the mind gets peace, digestion remains healthy
 saath hi immune system kii kshamta bhi tej hoti he

 Actually, Amit Shah was speaking at the Youth Parliament of India-2018 event in Gandhinagar
 isi dauraan unhone ye baaten kahin
 Shah also said that it is possible to take the country forward with the help of the youth
 congress par bhi nishaanaa saadhakaaryakram main bolte hue amit shah ne congress par bhi nishaanaa saadhaa
 He said, 'when we imagine India of 2025, we have to see what we inherited
 unhone kaha ki 2014 main jab pehali baar purna bahumat ke saathmodi sarkarbani tab 60 karod log aise the jinke bank acount nahin the
 There was no toilet, no electricity
 ek tabake ko lagata tha ki unke liye azaadi nahin ai he
 Shah further said that today in 4 years, the work of opening a bank account of every family in the country has been done
 4 lakh se zyada logon ko gas silendar mila he
 Today there is not a single village where there is no electricity
 arthtantr kii gaadi patari se utari thi, use chaar saal main hamane aage laane kaa kaam kiya he

 ye saare kaam 2024 ke bharat kii ore pehla kadam he

 According to the news agency Xinhua, Ashton said, 'we have made concrete progress on some issues
 kuch mukhya muddon par ab bhi matbhed hai jiske liye or samay va prayaas kii jarurat he

 is samjhaute ke tahat iran kuch pratibandhon se raahat ke badale main apni kuch parmaanu gatividhiyon par roak lagane ke liye taiyaar ho gaya tha
